# -*- ck2.scripted_effects -*-
# Written by zijistark via trait-notify.pl v1.03.1 on Tue Apr 30 16:26:05 2019 (Pacific)


#########################################
#  TRAIT NOTIFICATION SCRIPTED EFFECTS  #
#########################################


#### [1] Amateurish Plotter: amateurish_plotter ####
emf_notify_add_amateurish_plotter = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { trait = amateurish_plotter } }
		add_trait = amateurish_plotter
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
				character_event = { id = emf_notify.1 }
				clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
			event_target:emf_notify_receiver = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
emf_notify_remove_amateurish_plotter = {
	if = {
		limit = { trait = amateurish_plotter }
		remove_trait = amateurish_plotter
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
				character_event = { id = emf_notify.1001 }
				clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1001 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
			event_target:emf_notify_receiver = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1001 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		limit = { NOT = { trait = hajjaj } }
		add_trait = hajjaj
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
				character_event = { id = emf_notify.114 }
				clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.114 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
			event_target:emf_notify_receiver = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.114 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
